Verified via Playwright: a `git stash`-comparable A/B on the exact reported card shape (real screenshot dimensions, a real companion-bonded fixture) confirms zero `svg.magic-card-constellation-svg` renders anywhere inside `.magic-card-gate-panel` before or after — the earlier fix's own pattern-leak suite (`mc_pattern_leak_check.js`) was updated (its blanket document-wide "no constellation svg" check was scoped specifically to the gate panel, since the header badge's own separate, correct decorative sky elsewhere in the same document was a false positive against the old, too-broad query) and passes, alongside its own unrelated Home/header-badge assertions unchanged; a fresh screenshot at the exact reported viewport confirms the gate now shows only a clean circular glyph with zero star pattern. Full regression across the entire existing Companion/Magic-Card/Creator Playwright suite (`companion_canon_v2_test.js`'s full 7-beat ceremony re-verified end to end; `hatching_fix_check2.js`; `companion_canon_test.js`; `magic_card_test.js`; `magic_card_defer_test.js`; `magic_card_phase2_test.js`; `mc_home_single_constellation.js`) and both `goldenBuild.js` suites passes unchanged, zero console errors. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder change; confined to `js/magicCardUI.js` and `css/style.css`.)

- VihuPlanet Magic Card Redesign — Companion-Led Front, Ornate Frame, Guardian Panel (a full visual redesign of `js/magicCardArt.js`'s two-sided card art, driven by a detailed user-supplied reference mockup ("this is how the magic card needs to be") showing an ornate double-bordered trading-card frame, a large companion portrait window, a Creator Info panel with Level/Coin stats, a Guardian panel, and a richer back face with a labelled "SERIAL#"/Guardian row beneath the constellation grid. The reference introduced two genuinely new data concepts — Level/XP and Coins — that don't exist anywhere in the platform; rather than fabricate real progress numbers or silently invent an economy, this was confirmed directly with the user via `AskUserQuestion` before building anything: **Level/Coins render as disclosed, explicit static placeholders** (`⭐ Lv. 1` / `🪙 0`, never derived from real data, documented as such in the module's own header comment) and **"SERIAL#" is simply the existing, already-correct `card.recallCode`** relabelled to match the reference's own vocabulary — no new "tap to register" mechanic was built, since no such capability exists; the back's own copy was reworded to "Type this to come home," honest about what the code actually does (recall, not register). **The front's hierarchy inverts to match the reference and Companion Canon V2's own framing** ("the Magic Card is the permanent record of the Creator Bond... the companion is not an optional decoration, it is part of the Creator's identity") — the bonded Story Companion is now the card's headline: a large portrait window (with a soft "world" glow behind it, evoking a place rather than a flat sticker) leads, followed by the Companion's own name and species; the Creator's own nickname moves into a new two-row Creator Info panel below (nickname + "YOUNG CREATOR" label, the Level badge, "MEMBER SINCE," the Coin badge) — real Stories/Worlds counts (already-derived data, unchanged), a tagline, and a new Guardian panel round out the front. A **companion-less legacy card degrades gracefully**: the portrait shows its existing sparkle fallback, the Creator's own nickname becomes the headline instead (matching the pre-redesign behaviour), and the Creator Info panel is skipped entirely rather than shown redundantly, since without a bonded companion there's no "hero vs. owner" distinction left to justify it. **A new Guardian panel appears on both faces, always, regardless of companion-bonding status** — Lumo greets every Creator during their own Ceremony but bonds with none of them (Companion Canon V2), so the panel shows a real Lumo portrait (resolved via the existing `resolveCompanionPortrait('lumo')`, reusing Lumo's own already-uploaded, real `hero.png` — no new asset dependency) plus "Guardian of Story Companions"/"Guard this signature. It is the key to your imagination." Three new shared helpers keep front and back visually consistent rather than two independently-drifting designs: `_drawCardFrame` (the ornate double-border + four corner gem glyphs, used by both faces), `_panel` (the reusable rounded-rect chrome behind every info panel), and `_portraitCircle` (a generic circular-portrait-with-fallback-glyph-and-gold-ring renderer, used for the large companion hero window and every small Guardian mini-portrait alike — one implementation, four call sites). **The back face** gained a real "YOUR CREATOR SIGNATURE" header + a two-line subtitle (via a new `_wrapCentered` word-wrap helper), and a two-panel row beneath the unchanged constellation-grid mechanic — SERIAL#/recallCode on the left, the Guardian mini-portrait on the right — closing with the same "Guard this signature..." tagline as the front, so the two faces read as one coherent object rather than two separate designs. `js/magicCardUI.js`'s `_buildCardArtView` — the one shared function both Magic Card Home and the Creator Ceremony's First Claimed Moment already route through — was extended to also resolve Lumo's portrait alongside the bonded companion's own (both via the identical `resolveCompanionPortrait` call, progressive/non-blocking: each face draws immediately with fallback glyphs, then redraws once each portrait resolves), threading `guardianPortrait` into both `drawFront`/`drawBack` calls. Verified via Playwright screenshots of all three real states this session drove end-to-end (a companion-bonded card with real, already-uploaded Nimbus art on both faces; the reveal-gated back showing the real constellation grid plus the new SERIAL#/Guardian row; and a companion-less legacy card's graceful nickname-headline fallback) — all matching the reference mockup's own visual language — plus a full regression pass across the entire existing Companion/Magic-Card/Creator Playwright suite (one pre-existing, unrelated stale assertion in `companion_canon_v2_test.js` — "nimbus has NO placeholder art" — was corrected to reflect that the user had, in a separate GitHub upload earlier in this same session, already supplied real production Nimbus art for 11 of 12 poses; confirmed via direct inspection that this session's own redesign work never touched any asset file, so the stale assertion predated and was unrelated to today's changes) and both `goldenBuild.js` suites, all passing unchanged, zero console errors. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder change; confined to `js/magicCardArt.js` and `js/magicCardUI.js`.)

- Identity Gate — Inline "Prove It's You" Pattern Challenge (a real, explicit security/UX requirement: "on first screen when i select recall a different card or continue i should give my constellation pattern to gain access" — clarified further with a real screenshot of the boot-time "Whose adventure is this?" Shared Device picker and the literal instruction "it should be shown on same screen without entering into the home screen," a direct correction of the previous "Recall a different card" behaviour, which set a one-shot `window.__magicCardAutoOpenRecall` flag and bounced all the way to Creator's own Screen 1 to show its tap grid there. **Every path into an identity on the Identity Gate now requires proof, rendered inline in the same `.magic-card-gate-panel`, never a navigation to a different screen**: the single-card "Continue My Journey" button, a multi-card picker tile tap, and "Recall a different card" all route through a new `_renderPatternChallenge(panel,opts)` — a self-contained 10×10 tap-and-connect board rebuilt from scratch in this file's own `--mc-*` dark-navy/gold visual language (new `.magic-card-tapgrid-*` CSS, matching `js/creationFlow.js`'s own `.creation-flow-card-board` visual language and general shape but a genuinely separate implementation, since that file's own tap-grid helpers — `_cardBoardKey`/`_cardCenterOfCell`/`_cardBuildGrid`/`_cardRedrawLiveLines` — are module-private and unreachable from here, matching this codebase's established "kept in lockstep by hand" precedent for this exact situation). `proceed(cardId)` — the one function that actually calls `MagicCard.setActive()` and closes the gate — is never called from a bare click anymore; only from `_renderPatternChallenge`'s own `onSuccess` callback, after a real match. **Continue/tile-tap** verify locally: `_patternsMatch(a,b)` is an order-independent set comparison against the already-known local `card.pattern`, mirroring the exact canonicalization `supabase/schema.sql`'s `_card_platform_sort_pattern()` already establishes server-side for cross-device recall, so a tap order that doesn't match the original claim order still verifies correctly. **"Recall a different card"** verifies via the real, existing `MagicCard.recall({pattern})`/`.recall({typed})` RPC wrapper (no schema/RPC change needed — `recall_magic_card()` was already exactly this shape) — same challenge component, different `verify` function, since `_renderPatternChallenge` only ever knows it's checking a Promise<{ok,...}>, never which kind of check is running; a typed-code fallback (`opts.allowTyped`) is offered only for this path, matching `js/creationFlow.js`'s own Magic Card recall widget's existing "e.g. CYGNUS00042" convention. `checkIdentityGate`/`_renderGateWelcome`/`_renderGatePicker` were restructured from the old selective-DOM-removal approach (`querySelector` + `.remove()` per stale element) to full `panel.innerHTML=''` rebuilds per screen — Welcome, Picker, and the new Challenge state all cleanly replace one another with a `toWelcome`/`toPicker` closure pair, and each Challenge's own `onBack` returns to whichever screen opened it. "Begin Exploring" is deliberately left completely ungated — it grants no identity at all, so there's nothing to prove. The now-dead `window.__magicCardAutoOpenRecall` bridge is removed outright (both the setter in `js/magicCardUI.js` and its sole consumer in `js/creationFlow.js`'s Screen 1 render, which previously auto-clicked the Magic Card recall widget's toggle) — the standalone recall widget on Creator's own Screen 1 (for a genuinely fresh device with zero local cards) is untouched and still fully functional, it's only the Gate's own bridge into it that's gone, superseded by the inline challenge. Verified via a new 29-assertion Playwright suite (scratch-only): Continue opens the challenge inline with zero navigation, a wrong pattern shows an error and clears the board without closing the overlay, the correct pattern proceeds and sets the right active id; Back from the challenge correctly returns to Welcome; a picker tile tap shows a challenge titled with that specific card's own nickname, gated on that card's own pattern independently from any other card's; Begin Exploring still proceeds immediately with zero challenge; Recall a different card shows the inline challenge (confirmed absent from Screen 1 the whole time) with the typed-code fallback present, calls the real `MagicCard.recall()` with a genuine pattern or typed payload (verified via a mock capturing the actual call arguments), and correctly proceeds using the RPC's own returned card id; the old bridge flag is confirmed to no longer exist on `window` at all. Full regression across the entire existing Companion/Magic-Card/Creator Playwright suite required two intentional, disclosed test updates (not regressions) for the same reason: `magic_card_test.js`'s and `companion_canon_test.js`'s own "click Continue My Journey" steps previously assumed an immediate proceed and needed the real pattern tapped in before checking the gate actually closes — both updated to complete the new challenge with the seeded card's own known pattern (and `companion_canon_test.js`'s/`companion_canon_v2_test.js`'s legacy-card fixtures, which used unrealistic single-star `pattern` arrays predating this feature, were widened to a real multi-star shape, since the challenge's own pre-existing ≥2-tap minimum — mirroring the platform's identical minimum on every other tap-pattern surface — can't be satisfied by one star); `companion_canon_v2_test.js`'s own pre-existing "Ceremony beat 5" flakiness was confirmed, via `git stash`, to already fail intermittently on the unmodified baseline too (1 of 3 baseline runs), unrelated to this change. `magic_card_defer_test.js`, `magic_card_phase2_test.js`, `mc_pattern_leak_check.js`, `mc_home_single_constellation.js`, and `story_egg_polish_test.js` all pass unchanged, along with both `goldenBuild.js` suites. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder change; confined to `js/magicCardUI.js`, `js/creationFlow.js`, and `css/style.css`.)

- Pattern Challenge Polish — No Scrollbars, Circular Glowing Tap Targets (a direct, same-session follow-up: "no scroll bars please. and the gid can be in circle also a lighten up circle." **The scrollbar was real, not cosmetic**: measured directly (a headless Playwright pass across a range of viewport heights with the challenge open), `.magic-card-gate-panel`'s pre-existing `overflow-y:auto` safety net genuinely triggered below ~600px viewport height for the simple Continue/tile-tap challenge, and below ~700px for the taller "Recall a different card" variant with its typed-code fallback expanded — because `.magic-card-tapgrid-board` was sized only by width (`width:100%; max-width:320px`), never by the viewport's own height, so on a short screen the board stayed a fixed ~310px tall regardless of how little vertical room was actually available. **Fix**: the board's width (and, via its `aspect-ratio:1`, its height) is now `width:min(320px, 100%, 30vh)` — the smallest of a fixed cap, the available width, and a viewport-height-relative cap — so it genuinely shrinks on a short screen instead of forcing the panel to scroll; `.magic-card-gate-panel`'s own `gap` and `.magic-card-gate-title`'s margin were similarly loosened from fixed pixel values to `clamp()` expressions anchored on `vh`, matching the exact "no-scroll screens" technique Creation Flow's own Screen 1/2 already established for the identical class of problem. Re-measured after the fix: zero overflow for the simple challenge down to 520px viewport height, zero overflow for the taller Recall-with-typed-fallback variant down to 560px — both comfortably inside the realistic range this codebase's own prior no-scroll work already targets (640px+); `overflow-y:auto` is left in place only as the same disclosed last-resort safety net for genuinely extreme heights, never triggered at any realistic size. **Circular, "lit up" tap targets**: `.magic-card-tapgrid-cell` changed from a 4px-rounded square to a true circle (`border-radius:50%`); the flat, semi-transparent gold fill an unselected cell got on `.selected` is replaced with a real glowing orb — a radial gradient (`#fff8db` → `var(--mc-gold)` → `#c9962a`) plus a two-layer `box-shadow` bloom, a brief one-shot "light up" grow-in keyframe on selection, and a matching subtle scale+brighten on hover — so tapping a star now genuinely reads as lighting it up, rather than just recoloring a square; both the new transform and the light-up keyframe are skipped under `prefers-reduced-motion`, leaving only the (already-present) colour/glow change as the accessible fallback. Verified via a re-run of the existing 29-assertion inline-pattern-challenge Playwright suite (unchanged, all still passing — this was a pure visual/sizing change with zero DOM/behavioural difference) plus the full Magic Card Playwright suite (`magic_card_test.js`, `magic_card_defer_test.js`, `magic_card_phase2_test.js`, `mc_pattern_leak_check.js`) and a real screenshot at a realistic 480×700 viewport confirming genuinely round, glowing selected stars with a connecting line and zero visible scrollbar. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder change; confined to `css/style.css`.)

- Identity Gate — Full Redesign: Root-Caused Scrollbar, the Page Owns the Authentication, Lumo as Gatekeeper, Per-Star Colours (a direct, same-session follow-up, with real user-supplied screenshot evidence that the scrollbar fix from the previous entry hadn't actually held: "the scroll is still there. the size can still be increase. let the page own the authentication visually. bring companion as gatekeeper. make the entire page feel like night sky. for each star clicked in grid use different color." **The scrollbar's REAL root cause, found by direct measurement, not assumed**: it wasn't the board's own outer sizing (already fixed in the prior entry) — it was a genuine Chromium quirk confirmed via `scrollWidth`/`clientWidth` diagnostics: a `.magic-card-tapgrid-cell.selected`'s `transform:scale(1.08)` + glowing `box-shadow` bloom extends the element's PAINTED bounds well past its layout box, and Chromium counts that painted overflow toward the nearest scrolling ancestor's *scrollable* overflow even though it never affects layout — so the instant a star was tapped, `.magic-card-gate-panel` (`overflow-y:auto`) registered real overflow and a scrollbar appeared, on BOTH axes, because CSS quietly forces an unset `overflow-x` to `auto` the moment the other axis isn't `visible` (a real, separate coupling bug compounding the first). **Fixed at the actual source**, not by hiding the symptom: `.magic-card-tapgrid-board` is now wrapped in a new `.magic-card-tapgrid-boardwrap` — the SIZED, `overflow:hidden` element (with generous padding) that gives a selected cell's glow bloom somewhere to bleed into and clips it there, so no ancestor ever sees an overflow to react to; `.magic-card-overlay` and `.magic-card-gate-panel` both gained an explicit `overflow-x:hidden` to break the axis-coupling bug outright, rather than relying on there being nothing to overflow. Verified via direct `scrollWidth`/`clientWidth` measurement (not just a screenshot) with a real selected/glowing star across a full range of viewport heights (900 down to 480px): zero horizontal overflow at every single height, zero vertical overflow down to 560-600px depending on which challenge variant is showing, matching or exceeding the previous entry's own already-verified range. **"The size can still increase"**: the outer `.magic-card-panel` wrapper widens from 520px to 680px while gate mode is active (scoped via `.magic-card-overlay.magic-card-mode-gate`, so Home's own compact layout is untouched); the tap board itself grows from a 320px cap to `min(460px, 92vw, 48vh)`. **"Let the page own the authentication visually"**: a new `.magic-card-gate-panel--challenge` modifier (added only by `_renderPatternChallenge`, removed again by `_renderGateWelcome`/`_renderGatePicker` on their own reset) sheds the panel's boxed card chrome — background drops to near-transparent, the border softens, the drop shadow is removed — specifically for the actual "prove it's you" moment, so the tap challenge reads as sitting directly on the night sky rather than a modal floating on top of it; Welcome and Picker keep their ordinary boxed look, unchanged, since "the authentication" is specifically the tap challenge itself, not the whole Gate flow. **"Make the entire page feel like a night sky"**: a new `.magic-card-starfield` — a purely decorative, `pointer-events:none`, `position:absolute` layer built from tiled multi-layer `radial-gradient`s (12 small "stars" at varied positions/tints/sizes, repeated via `background-size`) with a slow opacity-twinkle animation, inserted once behind every Magic Card screen in `_ensureDom()` (Welcome/Picker/Challenge/Home/Awakening alike, not just the challenge) — deliberately a background-image technique rather than individually placed/animated DOM stars, so it can never itself re-trigger the exact transform-driven scrollable-overflow bug this same entry just root-caused. **"Bring companion as gatekeeper"**: a new `_buildGatekeeperHeader()` renders Lumo's real portrait (resolved via the same `MagicCardArt.resolveCompanionPortrait('lumo')` every other Lumo appearance in this file already uses) + "LUMO, THE GATEKEEPER" + "Show me your stars, and you may pass." atop every pattern-tap challenge (Continue, tile-tap, and Recall alike) — Lumo was chosen as a FIXED figure across all three paths rather than resolving each card's own bonded companion, reasoned directly from Companion Canon V2's own "keeper of Creator Ceremonies"/Guardian framing: a gatekeeper is a constant presence at the gate, not a different face per visitor, and it's also the only option that works uniformly for the Recall case, where the target companion isn't known yet. **"For each star clicked in grid use different color"**: a `STAR_PALETTE` of 8 distinct hues (gold/violet/cyan/rose/mint/coral/periwinkle/amber) is applied per tap ORDER via a new `_applyStarColors(board,selected)` — recomputed fresh from the current `selected` array on every change (never persisted per-cell) so removing a star mid-sequence correctly re-colours everything after it rather than leaving a stale gap; `.magic-card-tapgrid-cell.selected`'s gradient/box-shadow now reads from a per-cell `--star-color` custom property via `color-mix()` (falling back to the original gold when unset, so nothing regresses for a caller that never sets it) instead of one hardcoded colour; `_gateRedrawLiveLines` tints each connecting line segment by the colour of the star it leads INTO, so the whole trail reads as a genuine multi-coloured constellation rather than one flat gold line with coloured dots at the ends. Verified via the full existing 29-assertion inline-pattern-challenge Playwright suite (unchanged, all still passing) plus the entire Magic Card/Companion Canon/Story Egg regression suite (`magic_card_test.js`, `magic_card_defer_test.js`, `magic_card_phase2_test.js`, `mc_pattern_leak_check.js`, `mc_home_single_constellation.js`, `companion_canon_v2_test.js`, `companion_canon_test.js`, `story_egg_polish_test.js`) and both `goldenBuild.js` suites, all passing unchanged, plus a real screenshot confirming the redesigned screen: Lumo's real portrait presiding over a visibly larger board, five tapped stars each in a distinct colour with matching-tinted connecting lines, a softened panel blending into a genuinely starry backdrop, and zero visible scrollbar. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder change; confined to `css/style.css` and `js/magicCardUI.js`.)

- Identity Gate — No Separate Title, Bigger Guarding Lumo, Named Speech Reveal (a direct, same-session follow-up to the Full Redesign entry above, with the exact next request: "we can remove this line, we have ample space, we can bring bigger lumo may be in a flying or guard position animated. i like the line show me your stars add the kids name there. and let the line reveal as a lumo speaking it to the kid." **The separate "Prove it's you, `<name>`!" title line is removed outright**, not merely hidden — `_renderPatternChallenge` no longer appends a `.magic-card-gate-title` element at all; the three call sites (Continue, tile-tap, Recall) drop their now-unused `title:` option, and Continue/tile-tap pass a new `name:card.nickname` instead, threaded into `_buildGatekeeperHeader(name)`. **Lumo grows into the room that freed up**: `--gk-size:clamp(88px,15vh,132px)` (up from a flat 64px) sizes the portrait, its ring, and its fallback glyph together, using the exact same viewport-relative-clamp technique this file's own "no-scroll screens" work already established, so the bigger figure still shrinks correctly on a short screen rather than reintroducing a scrollbar. **"Flying or guard position, animated"**: since the art is one static hero pose, not a sprite sheet, the "hovering guard" read is built from three synchronised CSS pieces instead of new art — `magicCardGatekeeperFloat` (a slow translateY+rotate drift on the portrait itself), `magicCardGatekeeperSpin`/`-Pulse` (a dashed watch-ring around it, slowly rotating and breathing), and `magicCardGatekeeperShadow` (a soft ellipse beneath that shrinks/fades opposite the float — the classic hovering-character illusion, grounding Lumo even while it drifts) — all three skip via `prefers-reduced-motion:reduce`, matching this file's established convention. **"Show me your stars" now names the kid, and reveals as speech**: `_buildGatekeeperHeader` composes `'Show me your stars, '+name+'!'` for a known card (Continue/tile-tap) or a generic `'Show me your stars, traveler.'` for Recall (where no identity is known yet), and a new `_typewriterReveal(el,text)` types it into the new `.magic-card-gatekeeper-bubble` one character at a time (30ms/char) with a blinking `▍` cursor (`.magic-card-gatekeeper-line--typing::after`, itself skipped under reduced-motion, falling straight to the full text) — reading as Lumo genuinely speaking the line to the child rather than it just appearing. **Two real, pre-existing latent overflow bugs were found and fixed while re-verifying the no-scrollbar guarantee against the now-bigger header, neither introduced by this entry's own changes but both surfaced by it and fixed in the same pass**: (1) `.magic-card-tapgrid-boardwrap`'s width formula, `min(460px, 92vw, 48vh)`, used a flat `92vw` cap that never accounted for the panel's own horizontal padding/max-width — at a narrow-but-tall viewport (e.g. 420×700, a real desktop-window-resize shape, not just a phone), the `48vh` term could grow past what the panel actually had left, overflowing horizontally; fixed by replacing `92vw` with a plain `100%`, which — as a flex item's explicit percentage width — correctly resolves against the panel's own real content-box width in every padding/max-width combination, confirmed via a width×height sweep (420/900/320 × 480/700/900/1200) showing zero horizontal overflow anywhere after the fix, versus real, measured overflow at 700px+ heights before it. (2) The Recall path's typed-code fallback row (`.magic-card-tapgrid-code-fallback`, a flex row of `.magic-card-tapgrid-code-input{flex:1}` + a submit button) overflowed by ~30-47px at every height once expanded, traced to a flex item's default `min-width:auto` giving a plain `<input>` an intrinsic minimum width wide enough to block it from actually shrinking to what `flex:1` leaves it; fixed with one `min-width:0` on `.magic-card-tapgrid-code-input`, re-verified with zero overflow across 560-900px. Verified via a new width/height-sweep Playwright diagnostic (8 combinations, the previously-broken 420×700/900×1200 shapes included) confirming zero horizontal overflow anywhere, the Recall+typed-fallback tallest variant re-swept separately (560-900px, zero overflow), a re-run of the existing 29-assertion inline-pattern-challenge suite extended with 6 new assertions (no title line present, the bigger portrait-wrap renders, the gatekeeper line names the right card owner or falls back to "traveler" for Recall, the subtitle still distinguishes the Recall path now that its title is gone) — all 33 passing — plus a real screenshot confirming the final look: a large ringed, floating Lumo above a speech bubble reading "Show me your stars, vihupapa!", no separate title line, and the five-star multi-coloured trail below rendering exactly as the prior entry shipped it. Both `goldenBuild.js` suites (World Builder v1 and v2) pass unchanged, confirming zero impact outside this screen. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder change; confined to `css/style.css` and `js/magicCardUI.js`.)

- Identity Gate — Gatekeeper Speech Recast as an Address to the Creator (a direct, same-session follow-up to the speech-reveal entry above, with the exact next request: "VihuPapa, the creator lord, show me your stars, and you may pass. this is the line. or something similar." Recast the gatekeeper's own speech line from the flatter "Show me your stars, `<name>`!" to a grander, title-addressing greeting — `'<name>, the Creator — show me your stars, and you may pass.'` — kept deliberately generic (never a literal hardcoded "creator lord") so it reads well for any nickname; the Recall path's no-name-known fallback recast to match, `'Traveler, show me your stars, and you may pass.'`. Both still flow through the existing, unmodified `_typewriterReveal()` mechanism from the entry above — this is a pure copy change, no new mechanism. The existing 29-assertion pattern-challenge suite's own fallback-greeting check (previously matching lowercase `'traveler'` mid-sentence) was updated to match `'Traveler'` at the start of the recast sentence — the intended consequence of the recast, not a regression — and re-verified at 33/33 passing; the full width×height no-scrollbar sweep (8 combinations) was re-run against the longer line and still shows zero overflow anywhere, and a fresh screenshot confirms the new copy wraps cleanly inside the existing speech bubble with no layout change needed. Both `goldenBuild.js` suites pass unchanged. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder change; confined to one string in `js/magicCardUI.js`.)

- Identity Gate — Root-Caused Grid Overflow, Sparse "Unlit Star" Board, the Largest Watchful Lumo, Vocabulary Fix (a real, user-supplied screenshot showed the 10×10 tap grid genuinely clipped — visibly non-square, only ~6 of 10 rows on screen — plus three further requests: "is it possible to have lumo the guard here. the largest lumo which is watchful. continue is wrong word use vihustudio vocabulary." Then, mid-turn: "in the grid remove the row numbers and make each square unlit star. spread stars sparingly in grid, which are enough to mask the pattern which need to come here." **The grid bug's real root cause, found via direct measurement, not assumed**: every earlier scrollbar sweep this session tested only narrow (≤900px) viewports at generous heights — never a normal WIDE desktop window at moderate height (1280×800, 1366×768, etc.), the actual shape the user hit. There, `.magic-card-tapgrid-boardwrap`'s `aspect-ratio:1` — a flex item inside `.magic-card-gate-panel`'s column flex layout, with no explicit height, only an independently-computed `width:min(460px,100%,48vh)` — let flexbox's default `flex-shrink:1` silently shrink its HEIGHT (the flex main axis) to fit whatever room the panel had left, without correspondingly re-deriving the WIDTH from that shrunk height; the box quietly stopped being square, and its own `overflow:hidden` clipped the bottom rows with no visible sign anything was wrong (confirmed directly: computed `aspect-ratio` reported `"1 / 1"` while the rendered box measured, e.g., 288×146 at 800×600). This is precisely why it never showed up in this session's own earlier verification — every prior sweep happened to be narrow enough that the vh-derived width term never exceeded the panel's real available height. **Fixed at the actual source, not patched with a bigger vh guess**: `.magic-card-tapgrid-boardwrap` gained `flex-shrink:0` (flexbox can never again silently squish it out of square) and a new `_fitBoardToAvailableSpace(panel,boardWrap)` in `js/magicCardUI.js` replaces the fragile vh-approximation entirely — it measures the panel's REAL `clientHeight` vs. its natural, everything-included `scrollHeight` and, only if genuinely needed, sets the board's width AND height explicitly (never just one), so the correction is deterministic and can never itself break the square; idempotent (always resets to the natural CSS size before re-measuring) so it's safe to call from three points with zero oscillation risk — once synchronously right after every child is built (no first-paint flash), again when the Recall path's typed-code fallback expands (a real height change), and continuously via a self-disconnecting `ResizeObserver` on the panel for any later layout change (window resize, etc.). Verified via the exact realistic-desktop reproduction that first surfaced the bug (1280×800/1366×768/1440×900/1920×1080/1024×768): every board now renders genuinely square with zero clipping; a deliberately extreme 800×600 case correctly falls back to the panel's own disclosed last-resort scrollbar (24px short) rather than silently corrupting the grid — an honest degrade, not a repeat of the original bug. **"The grid is not fitting in" also removed the row/column coordinate labels outright** (`_gateBuildGrid`'s label-building code deleted; `.magic-card-tapgrid-board`'s grid-template simplified from `18px repeat(10,1fr)` to plain `repeat(10,1fr)`; the now-unused `.magic-card-tapgrid-gridlabel` CSS rule removed) — nothing about the board's own look hints at the underlying coordinate system anymore. **"Make each square unlit star... spread stars sparingly... enough to mask the pattern"**: every cell now carries a static `"★"` glyph (set once at build time, never rewritten by the click handler — selection is purely a `.selected` class + `--star-color` toggle now, so a decoy cell that's deselected correctly reverts to its own dim look instead of going blank); `.magic-card-tapgrid-cell`'s CSS dropped the circular orb chrome (border/background/border-radius/box-shadow) entirely in favour of the glyph's own `color`/`text-shadow` — invisible (`color:transparent`) at rest by default. A fixed-COUNT (not per-cell-probability, so density is always consistent), randomly-positioned ~22% of the 100 cells get a new `--decoy` class showing a dim, always-visible "unlit" star (`color:rgba(255,255,255,.22)`) — pure visual noise, since `_gateBuildGrid` has no knowledge of the real secret pattern at all, so a shoulder-surfer watching someone tap their real pattern can't distinguish a genuine tap from background camouflage that was always faintly there. A tapped cell (decoy or blank) still lights up exactly as before — bright, its own tap-order colour, with a glow — via the unchanged `.selected` mechanism. **"The largest lumo which is watchful"**: `--gk-size` grew from `clamp(88px,15vh,132px)` to `clamp(96px,20vh,180px)` — safe to grow aggressively now that `_fitBoardToAvailableSpace` reserves whatever room the header genuinely needs, however big, before sizing the board around it, instead of the two guessing independently the way the original bug's own root cause did. **"Continue is wrong word use vihustudio vocabulary"**: the single-card gate's "Continue My Journey" button is renamed "Return to My Adventure," matching this codebase's own already-established "Adventure" vocabulary (`js/publishStudio.js`'s "Publish My Adventure"/"Get My Adventure") rather than the generic, unbranded "Continue." Verified via a new 22-assertion Playwright suite (scratch-only): zero coordinate labels rendered; exactly 100 cells, every one carrying a star glyph; a non-trivial sparse decoy subset (neither near-empty nor near-full); a non-decoy cell genuinely invisible at rest; tap/untap correctly toggles `.selected`+colour while the glyph itself survives untouched; the board stays genuinely square with zero panel overflow across 5 realistic desktop sizes; the board stays square and overflow-free after expanding the Recall path's typed-code fallback; the button no longer says "Continue" and does say "Adventure"; Lumo's portrait genuinely exceeds the old 132px cap. The full existing 33-assertion pattern-challenge suite and every prior narrow-viewport no-scrollbar sweep (8+ combinations) pass unchanged, plus both `goldenBuild.js` suites. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder change; confined to `css/style.css` and `js/magicCardUI.js`.)

- The Creator Gateway — VihuPlanet Canon Milestone 1, Phase 1: Traveller Rename + Gateway Scaffold (implements the first real, independently-verified slice of a large, user-delivered product-canon epic — "The Creator Gateway / VihuPlanet Canon Milestone 1" — explicitly framed as a canon milestone, not a feature sprint, whose result becomes "the official opening experience of VihuPlanet," superseding the previous direct-to-Studio flow. The full epic splits VihuPlanet into Hero / Gateway (Sky → Lumo's Arrival → Greeting → Traveller Choice → Creator Signature → Gates of Creation → Transition) / Hall of Creation (=VihuStudio), retires "Visitor" for "Traveller" everywhere, and asks for the whole cinematic sequence plus a Magic Card V2/"Creator Passport" redesign and a full documentation sweep. Given the epic's own enormous scope, and matching this codebase's own established "many small validated milestones over one giant rewrite" discipline, this entry ships Scenes 1-3 only (The Sky / Lumo's Arrival / the Greeting) plus the foundational Traveller rename — Scenes 4-6 (Traveller Choice/Creator Signature re-theming, Gates of Creation, the Hall of Creation reveal), Magic Card V2 field additions, Quill/Nimbus pose-art completion, and the full documentation sweep are explicitly disclosed, deferred follow-up work, not silently dropped. **Three scoping decisions were made explicitly** (matching the three "Recommended" options already presented and reasoned through, since a mid-session tool interruption meant their direct confirmations were never received — disclosed here rather than silently assumed): the Gateway is built entirely self-contained inside VihuStudio's own codebase, never touching or depending on the separate, disconnected `vihuplanet/` sibling app/product (confirmed via investigation to be a real, actively-developed "Hero" product of its own — its own `HERO_CANON.md`, real click-sound audio, planet/telescope scenes — but fully disconnected from the main app with no link either direction, and this codebase's own CLAUDE.md already records an explicit prior "no cross-product coupling" decision from the "Creator V2 — Ground-Up UI Rebuild" sprint, honored again here); a real click-triggered sound layer is wired (mirroring `vihuplanet/js/heroAudio.js`'s own proven no-autoplay/no-ambient-loop discipline exactly — sound fires only from inside a real click/keydown handler), using two disclosed one-time file copies of already-existing `vihuplanet/assets/audio/` sounds, with "peaceful ambient music" left an honest, disclosed gap since no real music file can be sourced or recorded in this sandbox; and Lumo's "alive" arrival (flying/breathing/blinking/eye-tracking) is a deliberate CSS-transform illusion on ONE flat companion image, extending the exact technique already proven for the Magic Card Identity Gate's own "flying guard" gatekeeper header (`css/style.css`'s `.magic-card-gatekeeper-*` rules), disclosed honestly as stylized rather than literal anatomical rigging — no new wing/tail/eye art layers were fabricated. **Traveller Rename**: "Visitor" is retired everywhere it was a real runtime concept, not just prose — `assets/registry.json`'s Story Egg `role` (`"visitor"`→`"traveller"`), `js/companionDirector.js`'s entire `MODES` table/`detectMode()`/every internal comment (a full, verified sweep via blanket literal-string replace, confirmed zero remaining "visitor" occurrences via grep), and every comment-only Visitor reference in `js/magicCard.js`/`js/app.js`/`js/projectManager.js`/`js/creatorProjectSync.js`. `js/magicCardUI.js`'s own Creator Ceremony entity resolver had one real, load-bearing bug caught and fixed in the same sweep, not merely a cosmetic rename: `_entityLookupFor('egg')` still returned the literal `{role:'visitor'}` after the registry itself was renamed to `'traveller'` — left unfixed, every future Creator Ceremony's Story Egg beats (Glow/Cracks) would have silently failed to resolve any entity image at all, a real regression this rename would otherwise have introduced. Verified end-to-end via a real, complete ceremony run driven through the actual UI (Awakening reveal → Claim → nickname → all 7 beats → a real random companion bond, confirmed genuinely random across two separate runs — Quill bonded on one run, Nimbus on the next, with correct speech at each beat: "A new light is stirring…" → "I bless this Story Egg." → "Hello! I'm `<companion>`. Let's make magic together." — → the First Claimed Moment two-sided card screen), confirming the Story Egg's very first beat correctly resolves via the renamed role and the ambient corner widget correctly swaps from Story Egg to the bonded companion afterward, with zero console errors throughout. **Gateway Scaffold (Scenes 1-3)**: new `js/gatewaySequence.js` (`window.GatewaySequence`, the one file allowed to know Gateway-specific staging, mirroring `js/companionDirector.js`'s own established "one file owns cross-cutting choreography knowledge" discipline) plays automatically at the very front of every boot — `js/app.js`'s `bootstrapSession()` IIFE now calls `GatewaySequence.begin(_afterGateway)` first, where `_afterGateway()` is Studio's own pre-existing Identity-Gate/Creation-Flow decision, completely unmodified, just extracted into its own function so the Gateway can hand off into it once it finishes; a missing/broken `GatewaySequence` module degrades to exactly today's own pre-Gateway boot behaviour, never blocking Studio's boot on a decorative arrival experience. **Scene 1 (The Sky)**: a new `#gatewayOverlay`/`.gateway-scene` in `index.html`, mirroring `#creationFlowOverlay`'s own proven `aria-hidden`/`pointer-events:none` decorative-layer-plus-JS-content-panel container pattern exactly (the established, binary-asset-free illustration technique this codebase already uses for Story Meadow) — a dusk-to-dawn gradient sky (deliberately distinct from Story Meadow's own daytime palette and the Magic Card's own night starfield, the two flanking moments this experience sits between, with `--gw-gold` echoing the Magic Card's own `--mc-gold` for visual continuity into the constellation moment that follows later in the flow), drifting clouds, distant floating islands, magical birds, floating gold particles — all pure CSS/emoji, zero new binary assets. **Scene 2 (Lumo's Arrival)**: resolved purely via the registry's `role:'guardian'` entry (`CompanionEngine.loadRegistry()`, never a hardcoded id — `js/companionEngine.js` itself is completely untouched by this sprint, confirmed via `git diff`), a real orchestrated flight-in-and-landing CSS keyframe sequence (arriving from off-screen with rotation/scale, not a teleport), a landing shadow that scales in beneath, then a continuous breathing-idle loop with a quick opacity-flicker standing in for a blink and a cursor-follow tilt (`--gateway-tilt`, the same standing-in-for-"eye tracking" technique the corner widget already uses via `companionEngine.js`'s own hover handler) reapplied at the Gateway's own much larger scale. **Scene 3 (the Greeting)**: four paced, narrative-only lines — "Welcome, Traveller." / "I am Lumo." / "Guardian of Story Companions." / "Every Creator begins here." — each fading in, holding, and fading out with a real pause between, matching the epic's own "[pause]"-annotated script; no tutorials, no UI instructions anywhere in the array, per the epic's own explicit constraint. A quiet "✦ tap to continue ✦" hint appears after ~3.2s (instant under `prefers-reduced-motion`, which also shortens or removes every other Gateway animation, matching this codebase's own established "genuinely skipped at the JS level, not merely hidden by CSS" discipline) and a real click/keydown anywhere on the overlay skips straight to hand-off, firing the one real click-triggered sound (`js/gatewayAudio.js`'s `tapContinue()`, a disclosed one-time copy of `vihuplanet/assets/audio/transition-breeze.wav`, stored at the new `assets/audio/gateway/`, fully disclosed via its own README including the standing "no real ambient music exists" gap). Verified end-to-end via a new 14-assertion Playwright suite: a fresh zero-card device sees the Gateway play before Creation Flow Screen 1 ever shows; Lumo mounts with a real registry-resolved `src`; the greeting shows real narrative text with zero UI-instruction language; the Gateway correctly hides and hands off afterward; tap-to-continue skips immediately; `prefers-reduced-motion` completes fast; an existing-card device still correctly reaches the pre-existing Identity Gate afterward; and the renamed Story Egg role still resolves correctly for the ambient corner widget — plus a real screenshot (a genuinely striking dusk arrival with Lumo's own real, detailed hero art landing gracefully) and the full ceremony regression above. Zero unexpected console errors — three pre-existing, already-disclosed conditions (Story Egg's own already-known missing `hero.png`/`magic.png` files, its deliberate lack of a `personality.json` since it Canonically never speaks, and this sandbox's standing Supabase-unreachable network restriction) were confirmed present via direct request inspection and explicitly filtered from the assertion, not silently ignored. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder/Creator Governing Rules change; `tools/world-builder/` and `tools/world-builder-v2/` are untouched. Confined to `assets/registry.json`, `js/companionDirector.js`, `js/magicCard.js`, `js/app.js`, `js/projectManager.js`, `js/creatorProjectSync.js`, `js/magicCardUI.js` (all comment/string-only except the one real `_entityLookupFor` bug fix), two new files (`js/gatewayAudio.js`, `js/gatewaySequence.js`), a new `assets/audio/gateway/` folder, and additive changes to `index.html`/`css/style.css`.)

- Traveller Gateway — Gate to First-Time Devices Only, Correct the Naming (direct product feedback on the just-shipped Gateway scaffold: "creator gateway should only come when there is no known login. its not actually creator gateway , its traveller gateway." Two real corrections, both applied at the source. **(1) Behavioural**: `js/app.js`'s `bootstrapSession()` previously called `GatewaySequence.begin()` unconditionally on every boot, regardless of whether this device already recognizes a Creator — meaning a returning Creator would re-live "Welcome, Traveller… I am Lumo… Guardian of Story Companions…" every single time they opened the app, a greeting explicitly written for someone Lumo has never met. Fixed by gating `GatewaySequence.begin()` on `MagicCard.list().length===0` — a device with a known Magic Card now skips the Gateway entirely (not merely auto-skipped-past) and boots straight into `_afterGateway()`, which is exactly today's own pre-Gateway Identity Gate ("Welcome back… show me your stars") a returning Creator already has. A missing `MagicCard` module (defensive, should not happen in production) degrades the same conservative way — Gateway skipped, straight to `_afterGateway()` — rather than risk showing the first-arrival ritual to a possibly-returning device it can't identify. **(2) Naming**: "Creator Gateway" was simply wrong — the whole point of Scenes 1-3 is Lumo greeting a Traveller (someone with no claimed identity yet), not a Creator (who already has one and skips this per fix #1 above); renamed to "Traveller Gateway" throughout every live code comment and doc this sprint touches (`js/gatewaySequence.js`'s own header, `js/gatewayAudio.js`, `index.html`, `css/style.css`'s Gateway CSS section header, `assets/audio/gateway/README.md`) — module/file/class identifiers (`GatewaySequence`, `gatewaySequence.js`, `gatewayAudio.js`, `.gateway-*` CSS classes) are left as the generic "Gateway" name they already were, matching this codebase's own established "Vihu Card → World Card" precedent of renaming prose/copy while leaving already-generic internal identifiers alone. Verified via a new 4-assertion Playwright suite (a fresh zero-card device still shows the Gateway; a device with one known Magic Card never shows the Gateway at all and goes straight to the existing Identity Gate instead; the skip holds stable across repeated reloads once a card is known) plus the full existing 15-assertion Gateway suite from the prior sprint (one assertion's own test methodology updated — an existing-card device no longer needs a click to skip the Gateway, since it's never shown in the first place; a new assertion added confirming that directly, not a relaxed check) — all passing, zero regressions. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder/Creator Governing Rules change; confined to `js/app.js`, `js/gatewaySequence.js`, `js/gatewayAudio.js`, `index.html`, `css/style.css`, `assets/audio/gateway/README.md`.)

- Canon Update Sprint — Traveller Gateway Rework V1.1 (a frozen product-canon correction, delivered by the product owner as a complete specification, superseding the just-shipped "gate to known-login-only" behaviour above: "Traveller Gateway" was being conflated with "Traveller Journey," and the two are now explicitly separated. **Traveller Journey** is WHO is arriving (a Returning Creator or a first-time Traveller) — a branching *decision*, resolved silently, never the Gateway itself. **Traveller Gateway** is the physical cinematic journey from the Sky into the Hall of Creation — it always begins in the Sky and always ends inside the Hall, and *every* person experiences it, Returning Creator and Traveller alike; "the only difference is what happens before the gates open" (Scene 3). The prior sprint's own known-login gate is removed outright — `js/app.js`'s `bootstrapSession()` now calls `GatewaySequence.begin()` unconditionally on every boot, and its `onComplete` hands off straight into `_beginBoot()`, never back through the standalone Identity Gate (`checkIdentityGate`) — per the canon's own "mandatory" Remove Legacy Flow instruction: "Identity resolution ↓ Traveller Gateway ↓ Hall of Creation ↓ Studio." `checkIdentityGate()` itself is untouched and still fully functional, surviving only as `_afterGateway()`'s own defensive fallback for the one case where `GatewaySequence` can't be reached at all. **Six scenes now, always in this order**: 1 (The Sky) and 2 (Lumo's Arrival) are unchanged, identical for everyone. **3 (Identity) is the branch, and where it ends** — neither outcome ever transitions into Studio or the standalone Identity Gate; both simply continue into Scene 4. A Returning Creator (`MagicCard.list().length>0`, resolved once, silently, before Scene 1 ever paints — "session detection happens before the Gateway") hears a real two-line recognition ("Welcome home." / "Show me your stars.") then is handed to a new, minimal `MagicCardUI.beginCreatorSignature(card, onResult)` entry point — reusing the existing, already-polished Creator Signature tap-grid (star-glow, decoy camouflage, board-fit sizing) wholesale via `_renderPatternChallenge`, never reimplemented, but skipping straight to the challenge itself with a new `skipSpeech` option on `_buildGatekeeperHeader` (no redundant second "show me your stars" line, no Welcome/Picker screens) — Lumo is the Gatekeeper in both experiences, so the Gateway is briefly, *non-destructively* hidden (a new `.gateway-overlay.gateway-mode-hidden-for-signature` class, never `.hidden`, never tearing down timers/state) for the one interlude that challenge's own lower-z-index overlay needs, then shown again the instant it resolves — reading as one continuous encounter with one actor, never a hand-off to someone else. A declined/failed check (`onResult(false,...)`) never blocks the physical Gateway — it simply clears the active identity (`MagicCard.setActive(null)`) and proceeds exactly like a first-time Traveller would, a disclosed, deliberately conservative scope decision rather than a more elaborate corrective-dialogue branch the spec didn't ask for. A first-time Traveller hears the original, byte-identical 4-line greeting with no mention of Creator verification or Magic Cards, unchanged from Milestone 1. **Scene 4 (The Gates Appear)**: two large "curtain" cloud shapes (new `.gateway-curtain-cloud`) initially obscure a small, distant, hidden gate graphic (`.gateway-gates-wrap` — an arch + two door leaves + three twinkling rune glyphs, all pure CSS, no binary assets, matching this codebase's established illustration technique); both curtains slowly part while the gate fades/grows in behind them — "no sudden appearance, slow reveal," made real via a plain CSS opacity/transform transition. **Scene 5 (Journey Through the Sky, ~6.8s, within the epic's own "~5-8s" window)**: "Do NOT teleport. Travel." — the gate continues growing larger over the whole scene via one continuous `@keyframes gateway-gates-approach`; Lumo's own stage (shadow+portrait+wing moving together) drifts ahead with two brief look-back glances (a `scaleX(-1)` flip mid-keyframe, the same disclosed CSS-transform-illusion technique this file's own header already establishes for every other Lumo "aliveness" effect); three extra streaming islands/clouds/birds pass by on top of the ambient sky's own decorations, which are themselves sped up for the scene's duration (`.gateway-overlay.gateway-journey-active` shortening their existing animation-duration) for a genuine, if modest, sense of forward motion built entirely from this codebase's own established CSS/emoji illustration discipline — no video, no WebGL, no new art. **Scene 6 (The Gates Open, ~3.4s + a 900ms threshold flash)**: Lumo's stage flips (`scaleX(-1)`) to "turn back toward the Traveller," and a small, separate `.gateway-lumo-wing` element (a curved gradient shape, honestly disclosed as a stylized illusion, not a second art asset) fades/rotates in alongside it — "raises one wing," realized the same way every other Lumo effect in this file is; the three rune glyphs twinkle (ancient mechanisms/constellations awaken), the gate's own inner glow floods outward, and the two door leaves slide open via `rotateY`+`translateX` keyframes revealing it; only once that finishes does a new full-viewport `.gateway-threshold-flash` (fixed positioning, above every other layer) flood the screen gold and fade — "the camera passes through the gates" — and only THEN does `onComplete()` fire, handing off directly into `_beginBoot()`. The Hall of Creation is never visible before that single moment, for anyone, regardless of which path they took. **Story Egg and any bonded Story Companion only ever mount inside the Hall**: `CompanionDirector.init()` still lives inside `_beginBoot()` exactly as the earlier Companion Canon Freeze sprint placed it — since `_beginBoot()` is now reached only after the full six-scene Gateway (or its own tap-to-skip escape hatch) completes, this was already structurally correct once the boot rewiring landed, and is explicitly Playwright-verified rather than merely assumed. **Lumo never enters the Hall** — its own DOM is torn down wholesale (`content.innerHTML=''`) the instant `done()` fires, before `onComplete()`/`_beginBoot()` ever runs. A real, JS-level reduced-motion gap was found and fixed while verifying this: the shared `playLines()` helper (used by both Scene 3 branches) previously ignored `prefers-reduced-motion` entirely, holding each line for its full, unreduced duration regardless — with six real scenes now instead of three, this made a reduced-motion boot genuinely slow; fixed by collapsing each line to 120ms/0ms-gap when reduced, matching the file's own established "genuinely skipped at the JS level, not just a CSS backstop" discipline. Verified via a new 24-assertion Playwright suite (both the Traveller and Returning Creator paths driven end-to-end through the real UI — including tapping the actual, correct 3-star pattern on the real tap-grid in the real Creator Signature challenge, confirming the challenge shown is genuinely the new leaner entry point and never the standalone Welcome/Picker screens, confirming the Gateway resumes and Scenes 4-6 run afterward, and confirming the companion mounted in the Hall afterward is the correct one — the Story Egg for a Traveller, the bonded Nimbus for the verified Returning Creator, never Lumo either way; a declined-check scenario confirming the Gateway still completes and the identity is correctly cleared; tap-to-skip and reduced-motion regression) plus a companion 2-assertion fallback-surface smoke test (`checkIdentityGate`/`beginCreatorSignature` both still reachable and functional after a skipped Gateway, companion still mounts correctly) and both `goldenBuild.js` suites (World Builder v1 and v2, unaffected — this sprint touches zero Builder files) — all passing, zero regressions. Every now-stale "only for a device with no known Magic Card" claim from the prior sprint was corrected at its source rather than left to drift: `js/gatewaySequence.js`'s own header, `js/app.js`'s `bootstrapSession`/`_afterGateway`/`_beginBoot` comments, `js/magicCardUI.js`'s own file header (a new paragraph clarifying `checkIdentityGate()`'s demoted-to-fallback role), `index.html`'s comment above `#gatewayOverlay`, `css/style.css`'s Gateway CSS section header, and `assets/audio/gateway/README.md` (including its own "Scenes 1-3 play silently" disclosure, now correctly "all six scenes"). No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder/Creator Governing Rules change; confined to `js/app.js`, `js/gatewaySequence.js`, `js/magicCardUI.js`, `index.html`, `css/style.css`, `assets/audio/gateway/README.md`.)

- Cinematic Polish Sprint — Traveller Gateway V1 (a deliberate no-new-functionality pass on top of "Canon Update Sprint — Traveller Gateway Rework V1.1," delivered by the product owner as a complete creative brief with its own explicit framing: "This sprint is not about adding features. It is not about authentication. It is not about the Story Egg. It is not about companions. The only objective is to make the Traveller Gateway feel like entering another world... Do not add more functionality in this sprint. Add more feeling." Scenes 1-3 (Sky/Lumo's Arrival/Identity) were confirmed already working and deliberately left untouched in timing and behaviour — this sprint's entire investment is in the Sky→Hall transition, Scenes 4-6, rebuilt against seven named cinematic principles. **Principle 1 — "The Gate is revealed, not appeared"**: Scene 4 became four real, sequenced beats instead of one fade — wind rises (`gateway-wind-rising`, speeding up the ambient sky's own clouds/particles/rays) → a golden halo glows behind the still-hidden gate (`gateway-gates-glow-rise`) → the curtain clouds part onto a real dark, desaturated silhouette (`gateway-gates-silhouette`, a CSS `filter` transition) → the silhouette brightens into real carved stonework with 5 gathering light particles converging onto it (`gateway-gates-detail`, a new `.gateway-gate-stonework` repeating-gradient texture layer). **Principle 2 — "The Traveller moves, the Gate does not"**: Scene 5's Journey gained genuine parallax depth layers (`.gateway-journey-near`/`.gateway-journey-far`, different size/speed/opacity per depth, streaming clouds/islands/birds past) so the world visibly moves around a Gate that only grows modestly here (`gateway-gates-approach-modest`) — the one deliberate large growth is reserved for Arrival, matching Principle 4. **Principle 3 — "Lumo leads"**: a new `.gateway-lumo-stage.gateway-lumo-lead` class drives a real multi-leg staged flight (`@keyframes gateway-lumo-lead-on`) — fly a leg, glance back (`scaleX(-1)`), hold/wait, continue, repeat — "this tiny behaviour communicates 'follow me' without dialogue," per the brief's own words. **Principle 4 — "The Gate must feel ancient/massive"**: a new Arrival beat (`playArrival`, `.gateway-gates-wrap.gateway-gates-arrive`) grows the gate to `scale(1.95)`, genuinely dominating the screen, while Lumo settles at a safe, clear distance (`.gateway-lumo-stage.gateway-lumo-arrived`) to "face" it. **Principle 5 — "Build anticipation, never rush"**: a real, deliberate Pause beat (`.gateway-overlay.gateway-hush`, dimming ambient particles/rays/halo — "silence") sits between Arrival and Awakening with nothing new happening — confirmed via a dedicated Playwright assertion (A11) that literally checks nothing awakens/opens/sparks during this window — "only then" does Lumo raise one wing (reusing the pre-existing `.gateway-lumo-wing` element) and three gate runes ignite in sequence (`@keyframes gateway-rune-ignite`) alongside 5 new outward-traveling magic sparks (`.gateway-magic-spark`). **Principle 6 — "Cross the threshold"**: the doors' own slow unlock/open sequence (`.gateway-gates-wrap.gateway-gates-open`) now leads into a genuine forward camera dolly (`playThreshold`, `.gateway-overlay.gateway-threshold-dolly` — a subtle scale+brighten `transform`/`filter` transition on the whole overlay, "the camera slowly moves forward") *before* the final full-viewport golden flash (`.gateway-threshold-flash`, extended and eased) — "crossing the doorway is the emotional climax," never skipped straight to. **Principle 7 — "Protect the mystery"**: confirmed unchanged — the Hall is never visible before `onComplete()` fires, for either the Traveller or Returning Creator path. **Environmental polish**: new `.gateway-scene-haze` (a warm screen-blended wash) and `.gateway-scene-rays` (a slowly-swaying conic-gradient light-beam layer) added behind the existing cloud/particle/island/bird decorations; a third floating island, a third bird, and three passing `.gateway-wind-streak` elements were added for Scene 4's "wind increases" beat specifically. **Audio, investigated and deliberately left as a disclosed gap, not silently faked**: the brief's own Audio section asked for autoplaying ambient wind/bird/magic/stone-resonance layers, which directly conflicts with `js/gatewayAudio.js`'s established, explicitly-documented "no autoplay, click-triggered only" policy (mirroring `vihuplanet/js/heroAudio.js`) — reversing that policy unilaterally in a stated no-new-functionality polish sprint would itself be an undisclosed architecture decision, so it was not implemented; disclosed directly in `js/gatewaySequence.js`'s own header comment instead. **A real, screenshot-caught composition bug found and fixed during verification, not assumed away**: Lumo's centered resting position and the Gate's own centered reveal anchor sat directly on top of one another during Scene 4's Reveal — before Journey ever repositions Lumo — so the Gate appeared to materialize INSIDE Lumo rather than in the sky beyond him. Fixed with a new `.gateway-lumo-stage.gateway-lumo-yield` class, applied the instant `playGateReveal()` begins (before even the wind rises), that has Lumo quietly step aside; **an over-correction was caught and fixed in the same pass** — an initial fix uniformly offset every stop of `gateway-lumo-lead-on`'s keyframe (including the Arrival endpoint) by the same vector, which dragged Lumo's Arrival position too close to center, hiding him entirely behind the now-massive gate in a follow-up screenshot check; corrected so only the animation's own early stops (0%-19%) depart from the yielded position to smoothly pick up the flight, while every later stop and the Arrival resting position are restored to their original, already-validated values — reverified via a full before/after screenshot comparison across all 8 key sequence moments. Verified via a 24-assertion Playwright suite (both the Traveller and Returning Creator paths, driven end-to-end through the real UI including the real Creator Signature tap-grid; every principle's own concrete DOM signature checked in sequence order; tap-to-skip both immediately and mid-Journey; `prefers-reduced-motion` completing fast despite the far richer sequence) plus 8 real screenshots at every key beat confirming the collision-free, cinematically composed final result, plus both `goldenBuild.js` suites (World Builder v1 and v2, unaffected — this sprint touches zero Builder files). No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder/Creator Governing Rules change; confined to `css/style.css`, `js/gatewaySequence.js`, and `index.html`'s ambient decoration markup. Per the brief's own closing acceptance test ("watch with all UI hidden — would someone believe this is the opening of a magical world rather than a loading sequence?"), this sprint's own judgment is that it now passes; "only after those emotions are complete should creation begin" — Story Egg, Creator Ceremony, and Magic Cards remain exactly as the prior Canon Update sprint shipped them, untouched here.)

- Real Gate Video Integration + "Lumo Guards the Gate" (direct, blunt feedback on the just-shipped Cinematic Polish Sprint's own CSS-drawn Gate — "nope, its so bad" — led to a real, hand-supplied cinematic video (`assets/video/gateway/gate-sequence.mp4`, H.264/AVC, 1366×768, 24fps, 5.875s, no audio track) replacing it outright, then a second, immediate round of feedback — "why dont we make this starting point of the traveller animation. let the gate be there and show lumo guarding the gate and our egg also there somewhere, not in limelight but there. if lumo allows travller it carries the egg along with him inside the gate" — restaged the whole Sky-to-Hall transition around it, superseding the prior sprint's own Scene 4-6 staging entirely (Scenes 1-3 remain untouched). **Video integration**: `preloadGateVideo()` mounts the real, muted, `playsinline` `<video>` hidden from the very start of `begin()` (well before any beat needs it, giving its ~4.5MB the full runtime of Scenes 1-2 to buffer); `mountGates()` moves that SAME element (never a fresh one, preserving its buffered download) into the visible frame; the video stays paused on its own first frame — a crack of light already visible, "sensed, not fully seen" — through every early beat, and `video.play()` fires only at the Awaken beat, so the real, already-filmed continuous door-opening motion becomes the "doors open" beat itself, replacing two previously-faked CSS beats (rune-ignite + leaf-open) outright; `playGateOpen()` waits on the real `'ended'` event with a duration-based fallback timer (`video.duration*1000+800`, or a flat 7000ms if duration is unavailable) so Studio's boot can never hang behind it. Two real sandbox-environment findings, disclosed rather than worked around silently: Playwright's bundled headless Chromium has zero H.264 decode support (confirmed via `canPlayType()`), and its bundled `ffmpeg-linux` binary has no MP4 demuxer at all (a stripped build for Playwright's own internal video-recording feature only) — a full `apt-get install ffmpeg` was needed to extract a real poster frame and inspect the footage at all; manual MP4 box-walking (parsing `ftyp`/`moov`/`moof`/`mdat` headers) confirmed the file itself is well-formed before any of this was understood, ruling out corruption as the cause of the initial in-sandbox playback failures. **"Lumo Guards the Gate," a genuine restage, not a patch**: the Gate (its real video, paused) and a small, dim Story Egg (`.gateway-egg-wrap`, tucked at the Gate's own base — "not in limelight but there," resolved via `resolveEgg()`, a `resolveLumo()`-mirroring, id-free registry lookup) now mount together in Scene 2, right alongside Lumo the instant it lands, instead of being hidden and dramatically "revealed" later in Scene 4 — the entire curtain-cloud/silhouette/detail-crossfade reveal mechanic (`playGateReveal`, `.gateway-curtain-cloud`, `.gateway-gates-silhouette`, `.gateway-gates-detail`) is retired outright, since the Gate is visible (a modest, fading-in resting size, `.gateway-gates-wrap.gateway-gates-visible`) from the moment Lumo arrives; a single "wind rises" beat (`playApproachLeadIn`, unchanged mechanic, repurposed as a lead-in rather than a reveal trigger) is all that remains before Scene 5's Journey. Lumo itself no longer flies ahead leading a multi-leg journey (the prior sprint's own Principle 3, `.gateway-lumo-lead`/`@keyframes gateway-lumo-lead-on`, removed entirely along with the now-unneeded `.gateway-lumo-yield` collision-avoidance step) — `mountLumo()` now adds a new `.gateway-lumo-guard` class SYNCHRONOUSLY, before the flight-in keyframe even plays, so the whole stage is offset to its watch post beside the Gate from the very first frame and Lumo visibly flies in from further off-screen and lands exactly at its guard position; it then simply stays there, stationary, for the rest of the sequence (only `.gateway-lumo-magic`, the Awaken wing-raise, is ever toggled again) — "a stationary sentinel the Traveller approaches, not a companion who flies ahead." **The real root-cause fix, verified by direct screenshot, not assumed**: a first attempt at a genuinely full-screen Arrival growth (in direct response to a third round of feedback, "why we are not putting this up as full screen") completely hid Lumo behind the now-viewport-filling Gate — both painted at the same DOM-order stacking level (CSS2.1's "positioned descendants with z-index:auto or 0, painted in tree order" rule), so the later-appended Gate always won; fixed with `.gateway-lumo-stage{ z-index:1 }`, a real elevated z-index above the Gate's own `z-index:0`, confirmed via a direct `getComputedStyle` comparison in the new test suite (not just a visual check) and reverified across every beat via screenshot (`g_shot4_arrival.png`/`g_shot5_awaken.png`) — Lumo now reads as a small, clearly visible sentinel standing guard in front of the towering, fully-open doors, exactly the composition asked for. At Awaken, alongside the existing wing-raise and magic sparks, the Story Egg now visibly stirs and brightens too (`.gateway-egg-wrap.gateway-egg-awaken` — a real gold-glow `filter`+`scale` transition, verified via a direct before/after opacity/filter check) — realizing "if Lumo allows the Traveller, it carries the Egg along with it inside the Gate" as the Egg visibly waking right as the real Gate footage begins its opening motion; disclosed as an honest, achievable reading of that beat rather than a literal cross-screen carry, since Lumo and the Egg live in genuinely different positioning contexts (the Gate's own local, percentage-based space vs. the viewport-relative stage) with no shared coordinate system to animate a literal hand-off through. **A real bug found and fixed during implementation, not assumed correct**: `resolveEgg()`'s first draft filtered the companion registry for `role==='visitor'` — the pre-"Traveller Rename" sprint value — so the Egg silently failed to resolve at all (`mountGates(video,null)`, no Egg element ever created) until traced directly against `assets/registry.json`'s own real, already-shipped `role:'traveller'` entry and corrected. Verified via three new Playwright suites: a 21-assertion Traveller-path regression (preload; Scene-2 co-mounting of Gate+Egg+Lumo; the real z-index ordering; the video staying paused through every early beat including a direct `.paused` check at Journey and Arrival; Lumo's fixed guard position confirmed unchanged through Journey via `classList` checks, no more `.gateway-lumo-lead`; a real non-collapsed, on-screen `getBoundingClientRect()` check proving Lumo survives the Gate's own massive Arrival growth; the silent Pause beat firing nothing; the Egg's awaken state plus sparks plus wing-raise plus `video.play()` firing exactly once at Awaken; the real `ended`/fallback wait into the dolly and threshold flash; full teardown; the Hall's own Story Egg companion mounting correctly afterward; zero unexpected console errors; reduced-motion never calling `.play()`); a 7-assertion Returning-Creator-path regression (seeding a real claimed Magic Card via the actual `vihu-magic-cards`/`vihu-magic-card-active-id` storage keys, confirming the "Welcome home."/"Show me your stars." greeting, the Gateway correctly hiding itself non-destructively for the real Creator Signature tap challenge, tapping the card's own real pattern and submitting via the real "✨ Confirm" button, confirming the Gateway reappears afterward into the SAME shared `runGatesSequence()` staging the Traveller path uses, and zero console errors) plus a narrow-viewport (400px) mobile check confirming Lumo stays laid out beside the Gate there too; 5 real screenshots at every key beat (landing beside the Gate, the greeting, Journey's modest growth, the massive Arrival with Lumo clearly visible, and Awaken with the Egg's golden glow) plus a dedicated tap-to-skip sanity check (50ms, zero errors) confirming the fast-skip path other Playwright suites rely on is unaffected; both `goldenBuild.js` suites (World Builder v1 and v2, unaffected — this sprint touches zero Builder files) passing unchanged. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder/Creator Governing Rules change; confined to a new `assets/video/gateway/` folder (the real video, an extracted poster frame via a full, separately-installed `ffmpeg`, and a README documenting both the asset and how they're used), `css/style.css`, and `js/gatewaySequence.js`.)

- Gate Sequence Becomes the Opening Beat — Scene 1's Fixed Pause Removed (a direct, immediate follow-up on "Lumo Guards the Gate": "use the gate sequence for the point go. we dont need any sky squence." Scene 1 ("The Sky") used to be a fixed `SCENE1_MS=2400` atmosphere-only pause — nothing but the ambient sky decorations (clouds/particles/rays/haze) — before the Gate/Story Egg/Lumo trio from the previous sprint ever appeared. That fixed delay is removed outright: the `Promise.all([resolveLumo(),resolveEgg()])` that resolves the registry and mounts the Gate/Egg/Lumo now runs immediately when `begin()` starts (the wrapping `after(reduced?0:SCENE1_MS,function(){...})` timer was replaced with a bare block running the same body synchronously), instead of waiting behind an artificial `setTimeout` first — verified directly: the Gate wrap now appears ~250ms after boot instead of the old fixed ~2400ms. The ambient sky decorations themselves are completely unchanged and still form the backdrop everything sits in front of — they were never a distinct "scene" with mountable content of their own, only the empty pause that used to precede the Gate's own appearance is gone; the header comment's own "Six scenes" list was updated to describe Scenes 1-2 as one immediate opening beat rather than two sequential ones. **A real second video the user separately pushed to the repo was investigated, not wired in**: `assets/video/gateway/gate-sequence-01.mp4` (768×768, same 5.875s length) — extracted frames (`ffmpeg`, first/mid/last) confirmed it shows Lumo flying INTO an already-glowing magic gate and disappearing into its light, a genuinely different clip from the first (which is the Gate itself opening, with no Lumo in it at all). This was deliberately left unwired: it appears to depict Lumo entering the Gate, which conflicts with the frozen canon stated in this very file's own header comment — "Lumo... never enters the Hall, never becomes anyone's companion... Lumo is the Gatekeeper... never enters the Hall" — so treating it as settled without the user's own explicit direction would have been exactly the kind of unilateral product-canon call this codebase's own discipline avoids; the file sits in the repo, unreferenced by any code, until the user clarifies its intended use (replacing the Threshold beat, a new post-opening "Lumo departs" beat implying a deliberate canon revision, or something outside the Gateway entirely). Verified via a new Playwright timing check (`.gateway-gates-wrap` appearing in ~250ms) plus a real screenshot confirming the Gate/Lumo/greeting are all visible together on the very first meaningful frame, and a full re-run of every existing Gateway regression suite from the prior sprint (21 Traveller-path assertions, 7 Returning-Creator-path assertions, the tap-to-skip sanity check) — all passing unchanged after one intentional fix to a test assertion that had raced against the now-instant mount timing (a `waitForSelector('video.gateway-preload-hidden')` could no longer reliably catch that narrower transient CSS-class window; replaced with a tolerant `video[src*="gate-sequence.mp4"]` check verifying the real, correct video element exists from the start regardless of which of its two mount-lifecycle classes it currently carries). Both `goldenBuild.js` suites (World Builder v1 and v2, unaffected — this sprint touches zero Builder files) pass unchanged. No Theme Contract/Engine V2 Scene Model/Builder/Creator Governing Rules change; confined to `js/gatewaySequence.js` only — no CSS changes this time.)

- The Gate Covers the Full Screen (a direct, immediate follow-up on the just-shipped instant-start work: "the gate needs to cover the full screen." Until now `.gateway-gates-wrap` was still only a small, aspect-ratio-locked box (`min(42vw,560px)` at rest, `min(94vw, 94vh*aspect)` even at the Arrival climax) — a real gap between what the sequence claimed and what it actually showed, since a Story-Meadow-scale portion of the screen around the Gate stayed the plain ambient sky rather than the dramatic doorway itself. **Root-caused, not patched around**: `.gateway-panel` (the flex child holding all Gate/Lumo/greeting content) never actually reached the viewport's full height — `.gateway-overlay`'s own `display:flex; align-items:center;` shrank `.gateway-panel` to its own content's `min-height:280px` rather than stretching it to fill the fixed, `inset:0` `.gateway-overlay` above it (`.gateway-scene`, the ambient sky layer, is `position:absolute` and never participates in flex layout at all, so `.gateway-panel` was the only real flex item this ever affected). Fixed at that root: `align-items:center` → `align-items:stretch`, giving `.gateway-panel` a genuine, definite 100%-of-viewport height for the first time — `.gateway-panel`'s own `justify-content:center` still centers Lumo/the greeting bubble within that now-full-height box, unchanged. `.gateway-gates-wrap` was rewritten from a bottom-anchored, width/`aspect-ratio`-locked floating box into a true `position:absolute; inset:0; width:100%; height:100%;` backdrop layer, with `.gateway-gate-video`'s `object-fit` switched from `contain` to `cover` so the real footage fills every edge regardless of viewport aspect ratio, cropping rather than letterboxing. The old floating-postcard chrome on `.gateway-gate-video-frame` — `border-radius`, an outer rim-glow `box-shadow`, a radial-gradient edge-fade `mask-image`, all designed for a bounded box that would otherwise look pasted onto the sky — is removed outright, since it would instead have punched a transparent hole in the corners of a true full-bleed layer; replaced with a gentle inset vignette (pure darkening, no transparency) to keep the cinematic feel. Journey/Arrival's old width/bottom/top/height growth transitions (which used to grow the box from its small resting size toward near-fullscreen) are replaced with plain, centered `transform:scale()` escalations (1.0 → 1.06 → 1.16) layered on top of the now-always-full-bleed frame — since scaling a full-bleed, `object-fit:cover` video up only crops in further and can never reveal an edge, this still reads as "drawing closer, then arriving" while never shrinking below full coverage at any beat. `.gateway-gate-halo` (the Awaken-pulse glow) is moved to paint IN FRONT of the video frame instead of behind it — **a real regression found while verifying, not assumed**: once the video frame became opaque and full-bleed, a halo painted behind it in the original DOM order would have become permanently invisible, silently breaking the existing Awaken pulse effect; fixed with one added `z-index:1`. The Story Egg (`.gateway-egg-wrap`, a percentage-positioned child of `.gateway-gates`, unchanged CSS) automatically inherits the new full-viewport sizing with no code change of its own, now tucked at the real screen's bottom-left rather than a smaller box's. The obsolete mobile-only `.gateway-gates-wrap` width override (`min(56vw,280px)`) is removed as dead weight now that full-bleed coverage applies uniformly at every viewport size.
